msg:Advantages: The place is very large, the outdoor children's playground facilities are new and large, the green environment is good, and the breakfast road is not bad.

Disadvantages: The service is not up to par, and some facilities are not designed reasonably

1. Check in at the service center, not the regular main building lobby, and there is no service staff to inform in advance. I also waited for a long time at the front desk of the main building, and the staff was always on the phone.

2. Self-driving check-in, the service center and the main building are not on the same road, and there is no notification. It leads to running back and forth.

3. Because the venue is very large and the shuttle bus is dispatched in a mess, it took a long time to wait for one, and when there was a car that was not full at the service center, it was told to wait for the next one, which was too strange. There are cars coming and going, but they don't stop at the service center.

4. The bathroom door of the room opens outside, but there is no space under the door to put a floor mat towel, resulting in water at the door after washing, and the water that was not wiped dry caused me to slip.

5. If it is a parent-child hotel, there are no footstools and toilet seats for young children in the room, which is very inconvenient for children to wash their hands and brush their teeth.

Finally, let me talk about the price. The package I bought on Ctrip was 999+300=1299, which was not worth the price! When he arrived on the same day, the price was 980+, and the children's park on 4/6 in the children's package was free (if it was not free for guests staying in the hotel, then there would be no fun for parents and children)
It was dark in the park that night, and we couldn't camp the next day because it rained, so we had to give up the content of the package.
I don't want to go again.
